1 /* $Id: whirlpool.c 227 2010-06-16 17:28:38Z tp $ */
2 /*
3  * WHIRLPOOL implementation.
4  *
5  * Internally, we use little-endian convention, on the assumption that
6  * architectures which favour big-endian encoding are:
7  * 1. rarer
8  * 2. in decreasing numbers
9  * 3. able to decode little-endian data efficiently anyway
10  *
11  * The most common big-endian architecture is Sparc, and Ultrasparc CPU
12  * include special opcodes to perform little-endian accesses, which we use
13  * (see sph_types.h). Most modern CPU designs can work with both endianness
14  * and architecture designer now favour little-endian (basically, x86 has
15  * won the endianness war).
16  *
17  * TODO: implement a 32-bit version. Not only such a version would be handy
18  * for non-64-bit-able architectures, but it may also use smaller tables,
19  * at the expense of more lookups and XORs.
20  *
21  * ==========================(LICENSE BEGIN)============================
22  *
23  * Copyright (c) 2007-2010 Projet RNRT SAPHIR
24  *
25  * Permission is hereby granted, free of charge, to any person obtaining
26  * a copy of this software and associated documentation files (the
27  * "Software"), to deal in the Software without restriction, including
28  * without limitation the rights to use, copy, modify, merge, publish,
29  * distribute, sublicense, and/or sell copies of the Software, and to
30  * permit persons to whom the Software is furnished to do so, subject to
31  * the following conditions:
32  *
33  * The above copyright notice and this permission notice shall be
34  * included in all copies or substantial portions of the Software.
35  *
36  * THE SOFTWARE IS PROVIDED "AS IS", WITHOUT WARRANTY OF ANY KIND,
37  * EXPRESS OR IMPLIED, INCLUDING BUT NOT LIMITED TO THE WARRANTIES OF
38  * MERCHANTABILITY, FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE AND NONINFRINGEMENT.
39  * IN NO EVENT SHALL THE AUTHORS OR COPYRIGHT HOLDERS BE LIABLE FOR ANY
40  * CLAIM, DAMAGES OR OTHER LIABILITY, WHETHER IN AN ACTION OF CONTRACT,
41  * TORT OR OTHERWISE, ARISING FROM, OUT OF OR IN CONNECTION WITH THE
42  * SOFTWARE OR THE USE OR OTHER DEALINGS IN THE SOFTWARE.
43  *

46  * @author Thomas Pornin <thomas.pornin@cryptolog.com>
47  */

3278 #define DECL8(z) sph_u64 z ## 0, z ## 1, z ## 2, z ## 3, \
3279  z ## 4, z ## 5, z ## 6, z ## 7
3280 
3281 #if SPH_LITTLE_FAST
3282 #define READ_DATA_W(x) do { \
3283  n ## x = sph_dec64le_aligned( \
3284  (const unsigned char *)src + 8 * (x)); \
3285  } while (0)
3286 #define UPDATE_STATE_W(x) do { \
3287  state[x] ^= n ## x ^ sph_dec64le_aligned( \
3288  (const unsigned char *)src + 8 * (x)); \
3289  } while (0)
3290 #define LVARS DECL8(n); DECL8(h);
3291 #else
3292 #define READ_DATA_W(x) do { \
3293  sn ## x = n ## x = sph_dec64le_aligned( \
3294  (const unsigned char *)src + 8 * (x)); \
3295  } while (0)
3296 #define UPDATE_STATE_W(x) do { \
3297  state[x] ^= n ## x ^ sn ## x; \
3298  } while (0)
3299 #define LVARS DECL8(n); DECL8(sn); DECL8(h);
3300 #endif
3301 
3302 #define READ_STATE_W(x) do { h ## x = state[x]; } while (0)

3305  FUN(0); \

3307  FUN(2); \

3316  * First operation: XOR the input data with the first round key.
3317  */

3319  n ## x ^= h ## x; \

3332 table_skew(sph_u64 val, int num)
3333 {

3337 #define ROUND_ELT(table, in, i0, i1, i2, i3, i4, i5, i6, i7) \
3338  (table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i0, 0)] \
3339  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i1, 1)], 1) \
3340  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i2, 2)], 2) \
3341  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i3, 3)], 3) \
3342  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i4, 4)], 4) \
3343  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i5, 5)], 5) \
3344  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i6, 6)], 6) \
3345  ^ table_skew(table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i7, 7)], 7))
3346 #else
3347 #define ROUND_ELT(table, in, i0, i1, i2, i3, i4, i5, i6, i7) \
3348  (table ## 0[BYTE(in ## i0, 0)] \
3349  ^ table ## 1[BYTE(in ## i1, 1)] \
3350  ^ table ## 2[BYTE(in ## i2, 2)] \
3351  ^ table ## 3[BYTE(in ## i3, 3)] \
3352  ^ table ## 4[BYTE(in ## i4, 4)] \
3353  ^ table ## 5[BYTE(in ## i5, 5)] \
3354  ^ table ## 6[BYTE(in ## i6, 6)] \
3355  ^ table ## 7[BYTE(in ## i7, 7)])
3356 #endif

3358 #define ROUND(table, in, out, c0, c1, c2, c3, c4, c5, c6, c7) do { \
3359  out ## 0 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 0, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2, 1) ^ c0; \
3360  out ## 1 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 1, 0, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2) ^ c1; \
3361  out ## 2 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 2, 1, 0, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3) ^ c2; \
3362  out ## 3 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 3, 2, 1, 0, 7, 6, 5, 4) ^ c3; \
3363  out ## 4 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 4, 3, 2, 1, 0, 7, 6, 5) ^ c4; \
3364  out ## 5 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 5, 4, 3, 2, 1, 0, 7, 6) ^ c5; \
3365  out ## 6 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2, 1, 0, 7) ^ c6; \
3366  out ## 7 = ROUND_ELT(table, in, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2, 1, 0) ^ c7; \
3367  } while (0)

3369 #define ROUND_KSCHED(table, in, out, c) \
3370  ROUND(table, in, out, c, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)

3374  key ## 3, key ## 4, key ## 5, key ## 6, key ## 7)

3378  dst ## 1 = src ## 1; \

3388 void
3389 sph_whirlpool_init(void *cc)
3390 {
3391  sph_whirlpool_context *sc;
3392 
3393  sc = cc;
3394  /*
3395  * We want to set all eight 64-bit words to 0. A "memset()"
3396  * is not, theoretically, fully standard, but in practice it
3397  * will work everywhere.
3398  */
3399  memset(sc->state, 0, sizeof sc->state);
3400 #if SPH_64
3401  sc->count = 0;
3402 #else
3403  sc->count_high = sc->count_low = 0;
3404 #endif
3405 }

3407 #define ROUND_FUN(name, type) \
3408 static void \
3409 name ## _round(const void *src, sph_u64 *state) \
3410 { \
3411  LVARS \
3412  int r; \
3413  \
3414  READ_DATA; \
3415  READ_STATE; \
3416  ROUND0; \
3417  for (r = 0; r < 10; r ++) { \
3418  DECL8(tmp); \
3419  \
3420  ROUND_KSCHED(type ## _T, h, tmp, type ## _RC[r]); \
3421  TRANSFER(h, tmp); \
3422  ROUND_WENC(type ## _T, n, h, tmp); \
3423  TRANSFER(n, tmp); \
3424  } \
3425  UPDATE_STATE; \
3426 }

3432 /*
3433  * We want big-endian encoding of the message length, over 256 bits. BE64
3434  * triggers that. However, our block length is 512 bits, not 1024 bits.
3435  * Internally, our encoding/decoding is little-endian, which is not a
3436  * problem here since we also deactivate output in md_helper.c.
3437  */
3438 #define BE64 1
3439 #define SVAL sc->state
3440 #define BLEN 64U
3441 #define PLW4 1

3461 #define MAKE_CLOSE(name) \
3462 void \
3463 sph_ ## name ## _close(void *cc, void *dst) \
3464 { \
3465  sph_ ## name ## _context *sc; \
3466  int i; \
3467  \
3468  name ## _close(cc, dst, 0); \
3469  sc = cc; \
3470  for (i = 0; i < 8; i ++) \
3471  sph_enc64le((unsigned char *)dst + 8 * i, sc->state[i]); \
3472  sph_ ## name ## _init(cc); \
3473 }
